msg:I have stayed in this hotel many times. Although I have stayed in other hotels in Yizhuang, after comprehensive comparison, Grand Skylight is still the best personal choice. Here are a few reasons: First, the location. It is not far from Han's, Rail, and Tongren. They are all within walking distance. Second, the surrounding facilities are Han's Plaza, so eating and drinking will not be a problem. Besides, the hotel's own restaurant products are already very good. I ordered their beef twice, which was really good. Third, the hotel's fragrance is harmonious, the lobby and the room are unified, and the taste is in line with the hotel's positioning and theme, not abrupt or awkward. I give it a thumbs up manually. I personally think that the point that can be improved is that it is a bit complicated to order dishes from the hotel restaurant in the guest room. There was a QR code ordering before, but this time it was cancelled for some reason. Can it be restored? However, the flaws do not outweigh the merits. Overall, I still think it is the best hotel in Yizhuang!

The hotel also has meeting rooms of various sizes, and the equipment inside is very complete, which can meet various types of business needs. In particular, there are many well-known enterprises and institutions in the Yizhuang area. Staying in a hotel here can provide better support and convenience for business activities.

In addition, the transportation around the hotel is also very convenient. 從辦理入住開始, 從前台到客房服務, 均是體貼入微關懷倍至, 為緊張商旅平添了家的舒適。
此外, 酒店的25米四泳道游泳池, 和剛擴建置新的健身房, 為健身族提供了早七至晚十的健身機會, 實在物超所值。
客房內裝修舒適維護精心, 同樣無可挑剔。
酒店隨近停車方便, 公交便利,近核酸點, 出行方便。
再次為會員部, 前台, 客房餐飲部等點贊!!!
